That keeps the calculation in `decimal` arithmetic, which is commonly used when precision matters. If `id` is an integer, C# promotes it to `decimal` for this addition.\n\nIn practice, this is seed-data logic: it generates predictable, increasing values (for example, if `id = 1`, weight is `2.5`; if `id = 2`, weight is `3.5`). Get urgent packages that are not delivered yet\n    var urgentOpen = seedData.Packages\n        .Where(p =\u003e p.DeliveryPriority == DeliveryPriority.Urgent \u0026\u0026\n                    p.Status != PackageStatus.Delivered)\n        .ToList();\n\n3. Count packages by status\n    var statusCounts = seedData.Packages\n        .GroupBy(p =\u003e p.Status)\n        .Select(g =\u003e new { Status = g.Key, Count = g.Count() })\n        .OrderByDescending(x =\u003e x.Count)\n        .ToList();\n\n4. Find courier with the most assigned packages\n    var topCourier = seedData.Packages\n        .GroupBy(p =\u003e p.Courier)\n        .Select(g =\u003e new\n        {\n            Courier = g.Key.FirstName + \" \" + g.Key.LastName,\n            PackageCount = g.Count()\n        })\n        .OrderByDescending(x =\u003e x.PackageCount)\n        .FirstOrDefault();\n\n5. The base weight is `1.5` kilograms, and then the current `id` value is added, so each created object gets a different weight.\n\nThe `m` suffix is important in C#: it makes `1.5m` a `decimal` literal instead of a `double`. That keeps the calculation in `decimal` arithmetic, which is commonly used when precision matters. If `id` is an integer, C# promotes it to `decimal` for this addition.\n\nIn practice, this is seed-data logic: it generates predictable, increasing values (for example, if `id = 1`, weight is `2.5`; if `id = 2`, weight is `3.5`). Route definition  \n`app.MapGet(\"/api/packages/{trackingNumber}/status-async\", ...)`  \nCreates an HTTP GET endpoint at `/api/packages/\u003ctrackingNumber\u003e/status-async`.\n\n2. Parameters injected by ASP.NET  \n- `trackingNumber` comes from the URL path (`{trackingNumber}`).\n- `cancellationToken` is provided automatically and is used to cancel async work if the request is aborted.\n\n3. Async call  \n`await CheckPackageStatusAsync(trackingNumber, cancellationToken)`  \nCalls your async method to find package status.\n\n4. Not found response  \nIf no package exists, it returns `404 Not Found` with JSON:\n- `Message = \"Package not found\"`\n- `TrackingNumber = trackingNumber`\n\n5.
